 2598  git commit -m "the multiplication was solved by actually buiding rv32i toolchain with multilib inside of /opt/riscv/, this allowed me to compile factorial. The reason I can say this is because the linker options and cflags are different from the elf_maker makefile and the firmare_mriscv makefile, yet they both point to the same tool, I only pointed to the same tool after I knew factorial would compile and link. so this occured on 7/23 monday. and in my notebook 7/23 is when i did the rv32i build only script. and realized when i lookedinside of rv32i, i only had fesvr being installed and no toolchain. after doing ./build-rv32i.sh i think all of it came together"
